<review>I'd stopped into the shop a few days ago to grab a menu--I'd seen it on line, but one place said they didn't do take out, so I wanted to make sure. They do.

Yesterday, my husband went in to pick up lunch: kalbi ribs and wagyu beef plates with rice, kale salad, and a cabbage slaw with thin-sliced avocado on top.

Every bite was amazing! Tender, flavorful meats with delicious sauces, fresh and crispy salads with vibrant dressings--that are perfect accompaniments to the meat.

The plates were presented beautifully and weren't dripping sauce or grease (I hate sloppy to-go containers). It was very clear these guys care about the food and how they present it to customers!

It's a lovely little shop with friendly and informative staff, and it would be pleasant to dine in, when we can.

I highly recommend ordering from this gem!<//review><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMAUK9s6ilEBFJU6AEMeGQu3GccwqtZkciTRcJy=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMcpPGmXzNUdkdE1fFHcd-4Ue75uKf59MEGtep7=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</pics><Resp>None</Resp><Gmap_id>0x80dd2bea4865669b:0xf68dd64dbfe9db69<//Gmap_id></record></dataset><record>

<Name>Christopher Hyun< /Name><Time>1590531335438</Time><Rate>5</Rate>< review>
Buena Park, Calif (Orange County)

One of the best spots for chicken bowl type of eatings.

Service: Pleasant.

Food: OMG the chicken and wagyu beef is surreal.
Chicken: Typical fire grilled teriyaki. Bit salty for me and goes well with the house teri sauce & hot sauce.
Beef: Drool. Quality, softness and flavor is on point. Best beef bowl in America.
Mac Salad: For a $1 or $2 depending on size is worth it. I typically grab double mac. Whoever makes this for them deserves a cookie, pat in the back and a high five. It's commercialized/processed, but, not too obvious.
Rice: Korean style. Sticky. Preferred rice.
Salad: Sucks... Cause who raves about a damn salad?

Location: SE Plaza on Orangethorpe/Beach. Heavy congestion especially around Halloween. Adjacent to Fuddruckers.

Decor/Interior: Small. Limited seating.

Cost: $10ish. Appx $16 for legit fatties.

My favorite lunch spot =)
Happy eatings.
@cigarcpa<//review>
